v2 and v3 protocols. The v2 xDS API is deprecated and no longer supported as of version 1.31.2, with the `checkTransportVersion()` function in source/common/config/utility.h explicitly rejecting V2 API versions and only allowing V3 or AUTO.\\n\\n## Core gRPC Mux Implementations\\n\\nThe gRPC-based xDS subscription mechanism is implemented in three main variants:\\n\\n1. **Legacy Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The original GrpcMuxImpl class handles both state-of-the-world and delta-style xDS subscriptions. It manages bidirectional gRPC streams with v3::DiscoveryRequest and v3::DiscoveryResponse messages. The class maintains API state per resource type, handles request/response queueing, pause/resume logic, and TTL management.\\n\\n2. **Newer Delta Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The NewGrpcMuxImpl class specializes in delta xDS protocol, using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse. It implements more efficient incremental resource updates and on-demand resource requests.\\n\\n3. **Unified Template-Based Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The newest architecture provides a generic GrpcMuxImpl template that works with both SotwSubscriptionState and DeltaSubscriptionState, supporting both v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response and v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response pairs. This includes specialized classes GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta.\\n\\n## Subscription State Management\\n\\nResource subscription state is tracked through:\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements state-of-the-world xDS semantics where the entire resource state is sent on each update. It maintains version_info and nonce tracking for ACK/NACK protocol.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements delta xDS semantics where only resource changes are transmitted. Tracks per-resource versions and maintains requested/wildcard/ambiguous resource state maps.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy delta subscription state implementation for the older mux architecture.\\n\\n## gRPC Stream Transport\\n\\nThe **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h** template class provides the low-level bidirectional gRPC stream management. It handles stream establishment, message serialization/deserialization, rate limiting, and retry logic for v3 proto messages. The stream callbacks trigger discovery response processing in the parent mux.\\n\\n## API Version Enforcement\\n\\nThe **source/common/config/utility.h** contains the critical `checkTransportVersion()` template method that validates the transport_api_version field in ApiConfigSource. This function explicitly rejects V2 API versions and logs deprecation warnings, ensuring all subscriptions use only V3 transport protocol.\\n\\n## Factory and Integration Points\\n\\n1. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.cc**: Implements ConfigSubscriptionFactory to instantiate appropriate mux implementations (GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl, or XdsMux variants) based on runtime feature flags and configuration.\\n\\n2. **source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h/cc**: The main subscription factory that orchestrates creation of file, REST, gRPC, or delta gRPC subscriptions, with API version validation via checkTransportVersion().\\n\\n3. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: Contains the GrpcMuxContext structure that bundles configuration needed for all mux variants including async clients, dispatchers, service methods, and resource delegates.\\n\\n## Protocol Message Flow\\n\\nThe dual-version subscription handling follows this chain:\\n1. SubscriptionFactoryImpl::subscriptionFromConfigSource validates transport_api_version (V3 only)\\n2. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create instantiates the appropriate mux with v3 proto types\\n3. GrpcMuxImpl::addWatch queues DiscoveryRequest messages with v3 proto fields (version_info, response_nonce, resource_names)\\n4. GrpcStream::sendMessage transmits v3 proto messages via gRPC\\n5. GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse processes v3::DiscoveryResponse with nonce/version_info fields\\n6. SotwSubscriptionState/DeltaSubscriptionState generate next requests using v3 proto API\\n\\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) gRPC server subscribes to these mux implementations to receive resource updates across all types in a unified v3 proto stream.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":75,"oldLines":6,"newStart":75,"newLines":46,"lines":["     {","       \"repo\": It maintains version_info and nonce tracking for ACK/NACK protocol.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements delta xDS semantics where only resource changes are transmitted. Tracks per-resource versions and maintains requested/wildcard/ambiguous resource state maps.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy delta subscription state implementation for the older mux architecture.\\n\\n## gRPC Stream Transport\\n\\nThe **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h** template class provides the low-level bidirectional gRPC stream management. It handles stream establishment, message serialization/deserialization, rate limiting, and retry logic for v3 proto messages. The stream callbacks trigger discovery response processing in the parent mux.\\n\\n## API Version Enforcement\\n\\nThe **source/common/config/utility.h** contains the critical `checkTransportVersion()` template method that validates the transport_api_version field in ApiConfigSource. This function explicitly rejects V2 API versions and logs deprecation warnings, ensuring all subscriptions use only V3 transport protocol.\\n\\n## Factory and Integration Points\\n\\n1. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.cc**: Implements ConfigSubscriptionFactory to instantiate appropriate mux implementations (GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl, or XdsMux variants) based on runtime feature flags and configuration.\\n\\n2. **source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h/cc**: The main subscription factory that orchestrates creation of file, REST, gRPC, or delta gRPC subscriptions, with API version validation via checkTransportVersion().\\n\\n3. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: Contains the GrpcMuxContext structure that bundles configuration needed for all mux variants including async clients, dispatchers, service methods, and resource delegates.\\n\\n## Protocol Message Flow\\n\\nThe dual-version subscription handling follows this chain:\\n1. SubscriptionFactoryImpl::subscriptionFromConfigSource validates transport_api_version (V3 only)\\n2. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create instantiates the appropriate mux with v3 proto types\\n3. GrpcMuxImpl::addWatch queues DiscoveryRequest messages with v3 proto fields (version_info, response_nonce, resource_names)\\n4. GrpcStream::sendMessage transmits v3 proto messages via gRPC\\n5. GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse processes v3::DiscoveryResponse with nonce/version_info fields\\n6. The v2 xDS API has been fully deprecated and removed as of this version, with explicit validation in `checkTransportVersion()` that rejects any V2 API versions and only permits V3 or AUTO. Proto field renames between v2 and v3 (e.g., `resource_names` field in DiscoveryRequest) are handled automatically by the protobuf generated code; all source code exclusively references v3 message types.\\n\\n## Core gRPC Mux Implementations\\n\\nThe gRPC-based xDS subscription mechanism is implemented in three main architectures:\\n\\n1. **Legacy Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The original GrpcMuxImpl class handles multiplexed xDS subscriptions using the unified v3 gRPC stream. It maintains per-resource-type ApiState objects, manages bidirectional gRPC streams with v3::DiscoveryRequest and v3::DiscoveryResponse messages, implements request/response queueing with discovery request ordering based on Envoy's dependency graph, handles pause/resume subscription logic, and manages TTL-based resource expiration.\\n\\n2. **Newer Delta Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The NewGrpcMuxImpl class specializes exclusively in delta xDS protocol, using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse. It implements efficient incremental resource updates where only added/removed resources are transmitted, supports on-demand resource requests via requestOnDemandUpdate(), and manages per-resource versioning for fine-grained ACK/NACK semantics.\\n\\n3. **Unified Template-Based Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The newest unified architecture provides a generic GrpcMuxImpl template parameterized on subscription state type (S), state factory (F), and v3 proto message types (RQ=request, RS=response). This enables compile-time dispatch between SotwSubscriptionState (using v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response) and DeltaSubscriptionState (using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response), with concrete instantiations GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta.\\n\\n## Subscription State Management\\n\\nResource subscription state is tracked through:\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements state-of-the-world xDS semantics where complete resource state is transmitted on each update. Maintains last_good_version_info_ and last_good_nonce_ for tracking protocol state, generates v3::DiscoveryRequest with entire resource_names list, and implements heartbeat detection via empty responses with matching version_info.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements delta xDS semantics where only resource changes (additions/removals) are transmitted. Tracks per-resource ResourceState objects, maintains separate maps for requested_resource_state_, wildcard_resource_state_, and ambiguous_resource_state_, and generates v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest with only resource_names_subscribe/unsubscribe changes.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy delta subscription state implementation used by NewGrpcMuxImpl in older code paths, maintaining compatibility during the unified mux transition.\\n\\n## Watch Map and ACK Queue Management\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc**: Manages per-type-URL watch subscriptions, dispatching resource updates to all watchers of a resource type and tracking resource subscriptions via DecodedResource callbacks.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/pausable_ack_queue.h/cc**: Implements a priority queue for discovery request ACKs that respects pause/resume semantics. ACKs are held during pauses and released during resume to maintain protocol correctness while allowing subscription pausing.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/update_ack.h**: Defines the UpdateAck structure containing nonce and error_detail for protocol acknowledgments.\\n\\n## gRPC Stream Transport\\n\\nThe **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h** template class provides low-level bidirectional gRPC stream management. It handles stream establishment with exponential backoff retries, message rate limiting via TokenBucket for flow control, and invokes callbacks (onStreamEstablished, onDiscoveryResponse, onEstablishmentFailure) for state machine progression. The template is parameterized on request (RQ) and response (RS) proto types, with actual usage instantiating it for v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response or v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response.\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_failover.h**: Multiplexes primary and failover gRPC streams for high-availability xDS, presenting a unified stream interface while routing messages to either the primary or failover stream based on availability and health.\\n\\n## API Version Enforcement and Validation\\n\\nThe **source/common/config/utility.h** contains the critical `checkTransportVersion()` template method that validates the transport_api_version field in any ApiConfigSource-like proto. This function (lines 155-169) explicitly checks if transport_api_version equals envoy::config::core::v3::ApiVersion::V3 or AUTO, and returns InvalidArgumentError for any V2 value with a deprecation warning. This ensures all xDS subscriptions exclusively use V3 transport protocol.\\n\\n## Factory and Integration Layer\\n\\n1. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Implements GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, and AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory that instantiate appropriate mux implementations (legacy GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl for delta, or XdsMux variants based on unified_mux feature flag).\\n\\n2. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc**: Wraps mux implementations as Subscription interface, managing watch lifecycle, timeout handling, and adapting GrpcMux callbacks to SubscriptionCallbacks for configuration managers.\\n\\n3. **source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h/cc**: The top-level subscription factory orchestrating creation of file, REST, gRPC, delta gRPC, ADS, or collection subscriptions. Validates transport_api_version via Utility::checkTransportVersion() before creating subscriptions, preventing any v2 configurations from reaching the mux layer.\\n\\n4. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: Contains GrpcMuxContext structure bundling all initialization parameters needed by mux variants: async_client, dispatcher, service_method (sotwGrpcMethod or deltaGrpcMethod for v3 service definitions), local_info, rate_limit_settings, config_validators, xds_resources_delegate, and xds_config_tracker.\\n\\n## Proto Message Types and Field Mappings\\n\\nAll implementations exclusively use v3 protobuf messages:\\n- **State-of-the-world**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, version_info, response_nonce, resource_names, node, error_detail (request) and type_url, version_info, nonce, resources, control_plane (response)\\n- **Delta**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, response_nonce, resource_names_subscribe, resource_names_unsubscribe, initial_resource_versions, node (request) and type_url, system_version_info, nonce, resources, removed_resources (response)\\n\\n## Execution Chain for Discovery Requests\\n\\nThe dual-protocol subscription flow for v3 only:\\n1. The v2 xDS API has been fully deprecated and removed as of this version, with explicit validation in `checkTransportVersion()` that rejects any V2 API versions and only permits V3 or AUTO. Proto field renames between v2 and v3 (e.g., `resource_names` field in DiscoveryRequest) are handled automatically by the protobuf generated code; all source code exclusively references v3 message types.\\n\\n## Core gRPC Mux Implementations\\n\\nThe gRPC-based xDS subscription mechanism is implemented in three main architectures:\\n\\n1. **Legacy Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The original GrpcMuxImpl class handles multiplexed xDS subscriptions using the unified v3 gRPC stream. It maintains per-resource-type ApiState objects, manages bidirectional gRPC streams with v3::DiscoveryRequest and v3::DiscoveryResponse messages, implements request/response queueing with discovery request ordering based on Envoy's dependency graph, handles pause/resume subscription logic, and manages TTL-based resource expiration.\\n\\n2. **Newer Delta Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The NewGrpcMuxImpl class specializes exclusively in delta xDS protocol, using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse. It implements efficient incremental resource updates where only added/removed resources are transmitted, supports on-demand resource requests via requestOnDemandUpdate(), and manages per-resource versioning for fine-grained ACK/NACK semantics.\\n\\n3. **Unified Template-Based Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The newest unified architecture provides a generic GrpcMuxImpl template parameterized on subscription state type (S), state factory (F), and v3 proto message types (RQ=request, RS=response). This enables compile-time dispatch between SotwSubscriptionState (using v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response) and DeltaSubscriptionState (using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response), with concrete instantiations GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta.\\n\\n## Subscription State Management\\n\\nResource subscription state is tracked through:\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements state-of-the-world xDS semantics where complete resource state is transmitted on each update. Maintains last_good_version_info_ and last_good_nonce_ for tracking protocol state, generates v3::DiscoveryRequest with entire resource_names list, and implements heartbeat detection via empty responses with matching version_info.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements delta xDS semantics where only resource changes (additions/removals) are transmitted. Tracks per-resource ResourceState objects, maintains separate maps for requested_resource_state_, wildcard_resource_state_, and ambiguous_resource_state_, and generates v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest with only resource_names_subscribe/unsubscribe changes.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy delta subscription state implementation used by NewGrpcMuxImpl in older code paths, maintaining compatibility during the unified mux transition.\\n\\n## Watch Map and ACK Queue Management\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc**: Manages per-type-URL watch subscriptions, dispatching resource updates to all watchers of a resource type and tracking resource subscriptions via DecodedResource callbacks.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/pausable_ack_queue.h/cc**: Implements a priority queue for discovery request ACKs that respects pause/resume semantics. ACKs are held during pauses and released during resume to maintain protocol correctness while allowing subscription pausing.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/update_ack.h**: Defines the UpdateAck structure containing nonce and error_detail for protocol acknowledgments.\\n\\n## gRPC Stream Transport\\n\\nThe **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h** template class provides low-level bidirectional gRPC stream management. It handles stream establishment with exponential backoff retries, message rate limiting via TokenBucket for flow control, and invokes callbacks (onStreamEstablished, onDiscoveryResponse, onEstablishmentFailure) for state machine progression. The template is parameterized on request (RQ) and response (RS) proto types, with actual usage instantiating it for v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response or v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response.\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_failover.h**: Multiplexes primary and failover gRPC streams for high-availability xDS, presenting a unified stream interface while routing messages to either the primary or failover stream based on availability and health.\\n\\n## API Version Enforcement and Validation\\n\\nThe **source/common/config/utility.h** contains the critical `checkTransportVersion()` template method that validates the transport_api_version field in any ApiConfigSource-like proto. This function (lines 155-169) explicitly checks if transport_api_version equals envoy::config::core::v3::ApiVersion::V3 or AUTO, and returns InvalidArgumentError for any V2 value with a deprecation warning. This ensures all xDS subscriptions exclusively use V3 transport protocol.\\n\\n## Factory and Integration Layer\\n\\n1. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Implements GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, and AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory that instantiate appropriate mux implementations (legacy GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl for delta, or XdsMux variants based on unified_mux feature flag).\\n\\n2. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc**: Wraps mux implementations as Subscription interface, managing watch lifecycle, timeout handling, and adapting GrpcMux callbacks to SubscriptionCallbacks for configuration managers.\\n\\n3. **source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h/cc**: The top-level subscription factory orchestrating creation of file, REST, gRPC, delta gRPC, ADS, or collection subscriptions. Validates transport_api_version via Utility::checkTransportVersion() before creating subscriptions, preventing any v2 configurations from reaching the mux layer.\\n\\n4. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: Contains GrpcMuxContext structure bundling all initialization parameters needed by mux variants: async_client, dispatcher, service_method (sotwGrpcMethod or deltaGrpcMethod for v3 service definitions), local_info, rate_limit_settings, config_validators, xds_resources_delegate, and xds_config_tracker.\\n\\n## Proto Message Types and Field Mappings\\n\\nAll implementations exclusively use v3 protobuf messages:\\n- **State-of-the-world**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, version_info, response_nonce, resource_names, node, error_detail (request) and type_url, version_info, nonce, resources, control_plane (response)\\n- **Delta**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, response_nonce, resource_names_subscribe, resource_names_unsubscribe, initial_resource_versions, node (request) and type_url, system_version_info, nonce, resources, removed_resources (response)\\n\\n## Execution Chain for Discovery Requests\\n\\nThe dual-protocol subscription flow for v3 only:\\n1. SubscriptionFactoryImpl::subscriptionFromConfigSource validates via Utility::checkTransportVersion() that transport_api_version ∈ {AUTO, V3}, rejecting V2\\n2. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create instantiates GrpcMuxImpl/NewGrpcMuxImpl/XdsMux variants with v3 message types\\n3. GrpcSubscriptionImpl::start calls GrpcMux::addWatch with type_url\\n4. through a multi-layered architecture that exclusively uses v3 protocols. The v2 xDS API has been fully deprecated and removed as of this version, with explicit validation in `checkTransportVersion()` that rejects any V2 API versions and only permits V3 or AUTO. Proto field renames between v2 and v3 (e.g., `resource_names` field in DiscoveryRequest) are handled automatically by the protobuf generated code; all source code exclusively references v3 message types.\\n\\n## Core gRPC Mux Implementations\\n\\nThe gRPC-based xDS subscription mechanism is implemented in three main architectures:\\n\\n1. **Legacy Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The original GrpcMuxImpl class handles multiplexed xDS subscriptions using the unified v3 gRPC stream. It maintains per-resource-type ApiState objects, manages bidirectional gRPC streams with v3::DiscoveryRequest and v3::DiscoveryResponse messages, implements request/response queueing with discovery request ordering based on Envoy's dependency graph, handles pause/resume subscription logic, and manages TTL-based resource expiration.\\n\\n2. **Newer Delta Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The NewGrpcMuxImpl class specializes exclusively in delta xDS protocol, using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse. It implements efficient incremental resource updates where only added/removed resources are transmitted, supports on-demand resource requests via requestOnDemandUpdate(), and manages per-resource versioning for fine-grained ACK/NACK semantics.\\n\\n3. **Unified Template-Based Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The newest unified architecture provides a generic GrpcMuxImpl template parameterized on subscription state type (S), state factory (F), and v3 proto message types (RQ=request, RS=response). This enables compile-time dispatch between SotwSubscriptionState (using v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response) and DeltaSubscriptionState (using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response), with concrete instantiations GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta.\\n\\n## Subscription State Management\\n\\nResource subscription state is tracked through:\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements state-of-the-world xDS semantics where complete resource state is transmitted on each update. Maintains last_good_version_info_ and last_good_nonce_ for tracking protocol state, generates v3::DiscoveryRequest with entire resource_names list, and implements heartbeat detection via empty responses with matching version_info.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements delta xDS semantics where only resource changes (additions/removals) are transmitted. Tracks per-resource ResourceState objects, maintains separate maps for requested_resource_state_, wildcard_resource_state_, and ambiguous_resource_state_, and generates v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest with only resource_names_subscribe/unsubscribe changes.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy delta subscription state implementation used by NewGrpcMuxImpl in older code paths, maintaining compatibility during the unified mux transition.\\n\\n## Watch Map and ACK Queue Management\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc**: Manages per-type-URL watch subscriptions, dispatching resource updates to all watchers of a resource type and tracking resource subscriptions via DecodedResource callbacks.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/pausable_ack_queue.h/cc**: Implements a priority queue for discovery request ACKs that respects pause/resume semantics. ACKs are held during pauses and released during resume to maintain protocol correctness while allowing subscription pausing.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/update_ack.h**: Defines the UpdateAck structure containing nonce and error_detail for protocol acknowledgments.\\n\\n## gRPC Stream Transport\\n\\nThe **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h** template class provides low-level bidirectional gRPC stream management. It handles stream establishment with exponential backoff retries, message rate limiting via TokenBucket for flow control, and invokes callbacks (onStreamEstablished, onDiscoveryResponse, onEstablishmentFailure) for state machine progression. The template is parameterized on request (RQ) and response (RS) proto types, with actual usage instantiating it for v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response or v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response.\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_failover.h**: Multiplexes primary and failover gRPC streams for high-availability xDS, presenting a unified stream interface while routing messages to either the primary or failover stream based on availability and health.\\n\\n## API Version Enforcement and Validation\\n\\nThe **source/common/config/utility.h** contains the critical `checkTransportVersion()` template method that validates the transport_api_version field in any ApiConfigSource-like proto. This function (lines 155-169) explicitly checks if transport_api_version equals envoy::config::core::v3::ApiVersion::V3 or AUTO, and returns InvalidArgumentError for any V2 value with a deprecation warning. This ensures all xDS subscriptions exclusively use V3 transport protocol.\\n\\n## Factory and Integration Layer\\n\\n1. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Implements GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, and AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory that instantiate appropriate mux implementations (legacy GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl for delta, or XdsMux variants based on unified_mux feature flag).\\n\\n2. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc**: Wraps mux implementations as Subscription interface, managing watch lifecycle, timeout handling, and adapting GrpcMux callbacks to SubscriptionCallbacks for configuration managers.\\n\\n3. **source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h/cc**: The top-level subscription factory orchestrating creation of file, REST, gRPC, delta gRPC, ADS, or collection subscriptions. Validates transport_api_version via Utility::checkTransportVersion() before creating subscriptions, preventing any v2 configurations from reaching the mux layer.\\n\\n4. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: Contains GrpcMuxContext structure bundling all initialization parameters needed by mux variants: async_client, dispatcher, service_method (sotwGrpcMethod or deltaGrpcMethod for v3 service definitions), local_info, rate_limit_settings, config_validators, xds_resources_delegate, and xds_config_tracker.\\n\\n## Proto Message Types and Field Mappings\\n\\nAll implementations exclusively use v3 protobuf messages:\\n- **State-of-the-world**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, version_info, response_nonce, resource_names, node, error_detail (request) and type_url, version_info, nonce, resources, control_plane (response)\\n- **Delta**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, response_nonce, resource_names_subscribe, resource_names_unsubscribe, initial_resource_versions, node (request) and type_url, system_version_info, nonce, resources, removed_resources (response)\\n\\n## Execution Chain for Discovery Requests\\n\\nThe dual-protocol subscription flow for v3 only:\\n1. SubscriptionFactoryImpl::subscriptionFromConfigSource validates via Utility::checkTransportVersion() that transport_api_version ∈ {AUTO, V3}, rejecting V2\\n2. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create instantiates GrpcMuxImpl/NewGrpcMuxImpl/XdsMux variants with v3 message types\\n3. GrpcSubscriptionImpl::start calls GrpcMux::addWatch with type_url\\n4. GrpcMuxImpl::addWatch initializes ApiState::request_ as v3::DiscoveryRequest with type_url and node fields\\n5. SotwSubscriptionState::getNextRequestInternal populates v3::DiscoveryRequest with resource_names list and version_info\\n6. GrpcStream::sendMessage transmits v3::DiscoveryRequest via gRPC stub\\n7. GrpcStreamCallbacks::onDiscoveryResponse receives v3::DiscoveryResponse\\n8. GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse extracts version_info, nonce, and resources for watchers\\n\\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) gRPC server receives all these multiplexed streams and returns unified v3 proto responses across cluster discovery (CDS), endpoint discovery (EDS), listener discovery (LDS), route discovery (RDS), and other resource types.\"\n   205→}\n   206→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. It maintains per-resource-type ApiState objects, manages bidirectional gRPC streams with v3::DiscoveryRequest and v3::DiscoveryResponse messages, implements request/response queueing with discovery request ordering based on Envoy's dependency graph, handles pause/resume subscription logic, and manages TTL-based resource expiration.\\n\\n2. **Newer Delta Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The NewGrpcMuxImpl class specializes exclusively in delta xDS protocol, using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse. It implements efficient incremental resource updates where only added/removed resources are transmitted, supports on-demand resource requests via requestOnDemandUpdate(), and manages per-resource versioning for fine-grained ACK/NACK semantics.\\n\\n3. **Unified Template-Based Implementation (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/cc)**: The newest unified architecture provides a generic GrpcMuxImpl template parameterized on subscription state type (S), state factory (F), and v3 proto message types (RQ=request, RS=response). This enables compile-time dispatch between SotwSubscriptionState (using v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response) and DeltaSubscriptionState (using v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response), with concrete instantiations GrpcMuxSotw and GrpcMuxDelta.\\n\\n## Subscription State Management\\n\\nResource subscription state is tracked through:\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements state-of-the-world xDS semantics where complete resource state is transmitted on each update. Maintains last_good_version_info_ and last_good_nonce_ for tracking protocol state, generates v3::DiscoveryRequest with entire resource_names list, and implements heartbeat detection via empty responses with matching version_info.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Implements delta xDS semantics where only resource changes (additions/removals) are transmitted. Tracks per-resource ResourceState objects, maintains separate maps for requested_resource_state_, wildcard_resource_state_, and ambiguous_resource_state_, and generates v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest with only resource_names_subscribe/unsubscribe changes.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.h/cc**: Legacy delta subscription state implementation used by NewGrpcMuxImpl in older code paths, maintaining compatibility during the unified mux transition.\\n\\n## Watch Map and ACK Queue Management\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/watch_map.h/cc**: Manages per-type-URL watch subscriptions, dispatching resource updates to all watchers of a resource type and tracking resource subscriptions via DecodedResource callbacks.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/pausable_ack_queue.h/cc**: Implements a priority queue for discovery request ACKs that respects pause/resume semantics. ACKs are held during pauses and released during resume to maintain protocol correctness while allowing subscription pausing.\\n\\n- **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/update_ack.h**: Defines the UpdateAck structure containing nonce and error_detail for protocol acknowledgments.\\n\\n## gRPC Stream Transport\\n\\nThe **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_stream.h** template class provides low-level bidirectional gRPC stream management. It handles stream establishment with exponential backoff retries, message rate limiting via TokenBucket for flow control, and invokes callbacks (onStreamEstablished, onDiscoveryResponse, onEstablishmentFailure) for state machine progression. The template is parameterized on request (RQ) and response (RS) proto types, with actual usage instantiating it for v3::DiscoveryRequest/Response or v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest/Response.\\n\\n**source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_failover.h**: Multiplexes primary and failover gRPC streams for high-availability xDS, presenting a unified stream interface while routing messages to either the primary or failover stream based on availability and health.\\n\\n## API Version Enforcement and Validation\\n\\nThe **source/common/config/utility.h** contains the critical `checkTransportVersion()` template method that validates the transport_api_version field in any ApiConfigSource-like proto. This function (lines 155-169) explicitly checks if transport_api_version equals envoy::config::core::v3::ApiVersion::V3 or AUTO, and returns InvalidArgumentError for any V2 value with a deprecation warning. This ensures all xDS subscriptions exclusively use V3 transport protocol.\\n\\n## Factory and Integration Layer\\n\\n1. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/cc**: Implements GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory, and AdsConfigSubscriptionFactory that instantiate appropriate mux implementations (legacy GrpcMuxImpl, NewGrpcMuxImpl for delta, or XdsMux variants based on unified_mux feature flag).\\n\\n2. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/cc**: Wraps mux implementations as Subscription interface, managing watch lifecycle, timeout handling, and adapting GrpcMux callbacks to SubscriptionCallbacks for configuration managers.\\n\\n3. **source/common/config/subscription_factory_impl.h/cc**: The top-level subscription factory orchestrating creation of file, REST, gRPC, delta gRPC, ADS, or collection subscriptions. Validates transport_api_version via Utility::checkTransportVersion() before creating subscriptions, preventing any v2 configurations from reaching the mux layer.\\n\\n4. **source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_context.h**: Contains GrpcMuxContext structure bundling all initialization parameters needed by mux variants: async_client, dispatcher, service_method (sotwGrpcMethod or deltaGrpcMethod for v3 service definitions), local_info, rate_limit_settings, config_validators, xds_resources_delegate, and xds_config_tracker.\\n\\n## Proto Message Types and Field Mappings\\n\\nAll implementations exclusively use v3 protobuf messages:\\n- **State-of-the-world**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, version_info, response_nonce, resource_names, node, error_detail (request) and type_url, version_info, nonce, resources, control_plane (response)\\n- **Delta**: envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest and envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryResponse with fields: type_url, response_nonce, resource_names_subscribe, resource_names_unsubscribe, initial_resource_versions, node (request) and type_url, system_version_info, nonce, resources, removed_resources (response)\\n\\n## Execution Chain for Discovery Requests\\n\\nThe dual-protocol subscription flow for v3 only:\\n1. SubscriptionFactoryImpl::subscriptionFromConfigSource validates via Utility::checkTransportVersion() that transport_api_version ∈ {AUTO, V3}, rejecting V2\\n2. GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory::create instantiates GrpcMuxImpl/NewGrpcMuxImpl/XdsMux variants with v3 message types\\n3. GrpcSubscriptionImpl::start calls GrpcMux::addWatch with type_url\\n4. GrpcMuxImpl::onDiscoveryResponse extracts version_info, nonce, and resources for watchers\\n\\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) gRPC server receives all these multiplexed streams and returns unified v3 proto responses across cluster discovery (CDS), endpoint discovery (EDS), listener discovery (LDS), route discovery (RDS), and other resource types.\"\n}\n","numLines":206,"startLine":1,"totalLines":206}}}
